from agents.minimax import MiniMax

In [2]:
g = KuhnPoker3()
In [ ]:
agent_classes = [
    (CounterFactualRegret, {}),
    (MonteCarloTreeSearch, {"rollouts": 5}),
    (MonteCarloTreeSearch, {"rollouts": 5})
]
my_agents = {}
for i, agent in enumerate(g.agents):
    cls, kwargs = agent_classes[i]
    my_agents[agent] = cls(game=g, agent=agent, **kwargs)
In [4]:
g.reset()
while not g.done():
    g.render()
    print(f"Agent {g.agent_selection}")
    action = my_agents[g.agent_selection].action()
    print(f"Action {action} - move {g.action_move(action)}")
    g.step(action)
g.render()
for agent in g.agents:
    print(f"Reward {agent} = {g.reward(agent)}")

In [5]:
for agent in g.agents:
    if hasattr(my_agents[agent], 'train'):
        print('Training agent ' + agent)
        my_agents[agent].train(10000)
        print(dict(map(lambda n: (n, my_agents[agent].node_dict[n].policy()), my_agents[agent].node_dict.keys())))
    else:
        print(f'Skipping training for {agent} (no train method)')

In [6]:
agent_obj = my_agents[agent]

if hasattr(agent_obj, "node_dict"):
    for obs, node in agent_obj.node_dict.items():
        print(f"{obs} regrets: {node.cum_regrets}, policy: {node.policy()}")
else:
    print(f"Agente {agent} no tiene 'node_dict'. Tipo: {type(agent_obj).__name__}")

Agente agent_2 no tiene 'node_dict'. Tipo: MonteCarloTreeSearch
In [7]:
cum_rewards = dict(map(lambda agent: (agent, 0.), g.agents))
wins = dict(map(lambda agent: (agent, 0), g.agents))
reward_history = {agent: [] for agent in g.agents}

niter = 2000
for i in range(niter):
    g.reset()
    turn = 0
    while not g.done():
        print('Turn: ', turn)
        print('\tPlayer: ', g.agent_selection)
        print('\tObservation: ', g.observe(g.agent_selection))
        a = my_agents[g.agent_selection].action()
        print('\tAction: ', g._moves[a])
        g.step(action=a)
        turn += 1

    print(f'Game {i+1} - Rewards: {g.rewards}')
    for agent in g.agents:
        cum_rewards[agent] += g.rewards[agent]
        reward_history[agent].append(cum_rewards[agent]) 

    max_reward = max(g.rewards.values())
    winners = [agent for agent, reward in g.rewards.items() if reward == max_reward]
    if len(winners) == 1:
        wins[winners[0]] += 1
        print(f'Winner of Game {i+1}: {winners[0]}')
    else:
        print(f'Game {i+1} ended in a tie between: {winners}')

print(f'Average rewards in {niter} games:', dict(map(lambda agent: (agent, cum_rewards[agent]/niter), g.agents)))
print('Wins:', wins)

plt.figure(figsize=(14, 6))

# --- Gráfico 1: Reward acumulado ---
plt.subplot(1, 2, 1)  # 1 fila, 2 columnas, posición 1
for agent in g.agents:
    plt.plot(reward_history[agent], label=agent)
plt.title('Reward acumulado')
plt.xlabel('Partida')
plt.ylabel('Reward acumulado')
plt.legend()
plt.grid(True)

# --- Gráfico 2: Reward promedio hasta cada partida ---
plt.subplot(1, 2, 2)  # 1 fila, 2 columnas, posición 2
for agent in g.agents:
    avg_rewards = [reward_history[agent][i] / (i + 1) for i in range(len(reward_history[agent]))]
    plt.plot(avg_rewards, label=agent)
plt.title('Reward promedio hasta cada partida')
plt.xlabel('Partida')
plt.ylabel('Reward promedio')
plt.legend()
plt.grid(True)

# Mostrar ambos gráficos juntos
plt.tight_layout()
plt.show()

from nbconvert import HTMLExporter
import nbformat, os, time

def save_notebook_to_html(notebook_path=f"KuhnPoker3.ipynb"):
    """Guarda el notebook como HTML"""
    exporter = HTMLExporter()
    notebook = nbformat.read(notebook_path, as_version=4)
    html, _ = exporter.from_notebook_node(notebook)
    
    os.makedirs("notebook_exports", exist_ok=True)
    timestamp = time.strftime("%Y%m%d-%H%M%S")
    output_path = f"notebook_exports/KuhnPoker3_CFRMvsMCTS5vsMCTS5_{timestamp}.html"
    
    with open(output_path, "w") as f:
        f.write(html)
    
    return output_path
In [ ]:
save_notebook_to_html()
